 ’’ Despite appeals from various human rights organizations, Pakistan is ready to hang a criminal in a wheelchair
 25 agast ko sajaa dene kii is prakriya par aakhri sunwaayee honi he
 Murder convict Abdul Basit, 43, is handicapped and unable to reach the gallows
 saal 2009 main hi basit ko doshi qaraar diya gaya tha
 But within a year he suffered from TB, after which his entire body below the waist was paralyzed
 blike warrant ke baavjood talati rahi faanseeisi saal 29 july ko basit ke khilaaf blike warrant jari kiya gaya tha
 But his execution was postponed after the lawyers appealed
 basit ke vakil ne raashtrapati mamanun hossain ko dayaa yachika bheji he or daleel di he ki wheelchair par nirbhar ek shaks kofaansee denajel ke niyamon ke khilaaf hoga
 The execution administration is worried about how long a rope will be needed to hang Basit
 adhikariyon ke liye yah anumaan laga paanaa mushkil ho rahaa he kyonki basit kowhilchair samet faansideni he
 In such a situation, the noose has to be prepared according to the weight of him and his chair
 desh ke share bazaaron main agle saptaah vaayada or vikalp (emmendo) saudon kii paripakv ta avadhi puri hone ke kaaran utaar-chadhaav bana rah saktaa he
 The stock markets will be closed next week on Wednesday 27 March on the occasion of Holi and on Friday 29 March on Good Friday
 niveshak emmendo kii paripakv ta avadhi puri hone ke kaaran nivesh ke pantare badalenge or april 2013 ke liye nivesh ke faisle lenge
 The F&O deal will have to be settled on Thursday 28 March on the last business day of this month
 aagaamee garmi ke maheenon ko dekhte hue niveshak upabhokta tikaoo vastu, paryaton or yatra se sambandhit companiyon ko nivesh ke liye khangaal sakate hai
 In summer there is a holiday in schools in North India and people plan tours with family, due to which the income of companies engaged in these businesses increases during this period
 yahi nahin is avadhi main air condishnar, cooler, pankhe jaise utpaada banane vaali companiyon ko bhi adhik aay hoti he
 Therefore, in order to reap the profits from June to October, investments can be made in companies related to these businesses
 bazaar main bade paimaane par sheyaron kii aapurti ke kaaran sheyaron kii keemton main aam taur par oochaal aane kii ummid nahin lagaai ja sakati he, kyonki bazaar niamak bhartiya pratibhuti evam vinimay board (sebi) ke disha-nirdeshon or samay seemaa ke tahat nijee or sarkari kshetra kii soochibaddh companiyon ke june se agast tak companiyon kii 10 se 25 fisadi hissedari aam niveshkon ko deni he
 In the process, there will be a flood of stocks in the market and prices cannot be expected to climb upwards
 is maah shuukravaar 22 march se sansad main chaalu bajet satr kaa madhyavkaash ho gaya
 The session will then start from 22 April 2013, which will run till 10 May
 tippaniyan The government is going to consider several important Bills in the current budget session

 Investments can also lead to far-reaching decisions for many stocks due to the passage or absence of these bills or the inclination of the government and the opposition
